 According to Indian time, the solar eclipse will start at around 10
25 pm tonight
 12 bajkar 53 minute par grahan apane madhya main hoga or raat 3 bajkar 21 minute par grahan khatm ho jayega
 Often people ask what is a solar eclipse, then we give you the answer
 asal main prithvi apni dhuree par gumti he iske saath hi saath vah soramandal main surya ke chakkar bhi lagaati he
 At the same time, the Earth has its own satellite that is the moon or moon
 chand prithvi ke chakkar lagata he
 So whenever the moon moves on its axis between the sun and the earth, the sun stops appearing on the earth
 yah aanshik yaa purna rup se hota he
 This is the only astronomical event called solar eclipse
 is khagoleey sthiti main surya, chandramaa or prithvi teenon ek sidhi rekha main hote hai
